		enable_equipments = {

		}

		path = {

		}
		path = {
			leads_to_tech = early_sloop
			research_cost_coeff = 1
		}

		dependencies = {
			tech_naval_mtg_explosive_shells = 1
		}

		research_cost = 0.15
		start_year = 1800
		folder = {
			name = mtg_capital_folder
			position = { x = 14 y = @1800 }
		}

		categories = {
			naval_equipment
			naval_mtg_capital_ship_tech
			naval_mtg_gunboat_tech
			naval_mtg_gunboat_hulls_tech
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				afr_is_tribal = yes
				date < 1875.1.1
			}
			modifier = { factor = 0 num_of_naval_factories < 1 }
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				num_of_naval_factories > 5
			}
		}
	}
